implemented through a sophisticated class isolation and dependency injection architecture located primarily in the connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ package and related connect/api package.\\n\\n**Core Plugin Loading Infrastructure:**\\nThe system uses three key classloaders: PluginClassLoader (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java) extends URLClassLoader and loads plugin classes with isolation, DelegatingClassLoader (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java) extends URLClassLoader to coordinate plugin loading, and ClassLoaderFactory (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java) which implements PluginClassLoaderFactory (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoaderFactory.java) to create classloader instances.\\n\\n**Plugin Scanning via Reflection:**\\nPlugin discovery uses two parallel scanning mechanisms: ReflectionScanner (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java) uses ClassGraph library with reflection to scan all classes implementing plugin interfaces, and ServiceLoaderScanner (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java) uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism for META-INF/services discovery. Both extend PluginScanner (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java) and return PluginScanResult (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java) containing discovered plugin descriptors.\\n\\n**Plugin Descriptors and Type System:**\\nEach discovered plugin is represented as a PluginDesc (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java) generic descriptor containing class information and version metadata. PluginType (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java) enum defines supported plugin categories: SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, and CONNECTOR_CLIENT_POLICY. PluginSource (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java) record represents a plugin location with its associated classloader and URLs.\\n\\n**Interface-Based Dependency Injection:**\\nThe system supports dependency injection through standard Java interfaces defined in connect/api. Core connector interfaces are Connector (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java) base interface, SinkConnector (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java) and SourceConnector (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java) for data movement. Serialization plugins include Converter (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java) for schema and payload conversion, and HeaderConverter (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java) for header conversion.\\n\\nTransformation plugins include Transformation (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java) for record transformations, and Predicate (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java) for conditional transformation application. Extension plugins include ConnectRestExtension (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java) registered with ConnectRestExtensionContext (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtensionContext.java), ConfigProvider (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/provider/ConfigProvider.java) for external configuration, and ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java) for enforcing client configuration policies.\\n\\n**Plugin Management and Utility Classes:**\\nThe Plugins class (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) is the main facade managing plugin initialization, discovery, and instantiation. PluginUtils (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) provides helper methods including shouldLoadInIsolation() for determining isolation requirements, isConcrete() for validation, and pluginLocations() for path parsing.
